CC   -!- FUNCTION: [N-terminal protease]: Leader cysteine autoprotease that
CC       cleaves itself from the nascent polyprotein during translation of the
CC       viral mRNA. Once released, plays a role in the inhibition of host
CC       innate immune response by interacting with host IRF3 and inducing its
CC       proteasomal degradation (PubMed:17531282).
CC       {ECO:0000269|PubMed:17531282}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: [Capsid protein C]: Packages viral RNA to form a viral
CC       nucleocapsid and thereby protects viral RNA. Also plays a role in
CC       transcription regulation. Protects the incoming virus against IFN-
CC       induced effectors. {ECO:0000250|UniProtKB:P19712}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: [E(rns) glycoprotein]: Initial binding to target cell
CC       probably involves interaction of E(rns) with glycosaminoglycans
CC       (PubMed:10644844). Also possesses intrinsic ribonuclease (RNase)
CC       activity that can inhibit the production of type I interferon and
CC       assist in the development of persistent infections (By similarity).
CC       {ECO:0000250|UniProtKB:Q96662, ECO:0000269|PubMed:10644844}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: [Envelope glycoprotein E1]: E1 and/or E2 are probably
CC       responsible of cell attachment with CD46 and subsequent fusion after
CC       internalization of the virion by endocytosis.
CC       {ECO:0000305|PubMed:14747544}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: [Envelope glycoprotein E2]: E1 and/or E2 are probably
CC       responsible of cell attachment with CD46 and subsequent fusion after
CC       internalization of the virion by endocytosis (Probable). Probably
CC       functions as a coeffector of fusion providing structural integrity to
CC       the fusion complex and possibly controlling exposure of the fusion
CC       motif in E1 (PubMed:23569276). {ECO:0000269|PubMed:23569276,
CC       ECO:0000305|PubMed:14747544}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: [Viroporin p7]: Plays an essential role in the virus
CC       replication cycle by acting as a viroporin (By similarity). Forms ion
CC       conductive pores, which alters the cell permeability allowing the
CC       transport of ions and other small molecules (By similarity). Forms a
CC       leader sequence to properly orient NS2 in the membrane.
CC       {ECO:0000250|UniProtKB:P19712}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: [Non-structural protein 2-3]: Uncleaved NS2-3 is required for
CC       production of infectious virus. {ECO:0000269|PubMed:14963137}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: [Cysteine protease NS2]: Plays a role in the regulation of
CC       viral RNA replication. {ECO:0000250|UniProtKB:P19712}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: [Serine protease NS3]: Multifunctional protein that contains
CC       an N-terminal protease and a C-terminal helicase, playing essential
CC       roles in viral polyprotein processing and viral genome replication. The
CC       chymotrypsin-like serine protease activity utilizes NS4A as an
CC       essential cofactor and catalyzes the cleavage of the polyprotein
CC       leading to the release of NS4A, NS4B, NS5A, and NS5B. Interacts with
CC       NS5B to enhance RNA-dependent RNA polymerase activity.
CC       {ECO:0000250|UniProtKB:P19712}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: [Non-structural protein 4A]: Acts as a cofactor for the NS3
CC       protease activity. {ECO:0000250|UniProtKB:P19712}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: [Non-structural protein 4B]: Induces a specific membrane
CC       alteration that serves as a scaffold for the virus replication complex
CC       (By similarity). Plays a role in the inhibition of host innate immune
CC       response by inhibiting RIGI/IFIH1-mediated IFN-beta production
CC       (PubMed:34097933). {ECO:0000250|UniProtKB:P19712,
CC       ECO:0000269|PubMed:34097933}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: [RNA-directed RNA polymerase]: Replicates the viral (+) and
CC       (-) genome. Initiates the primer-independent RNA replication via a de
CC       novo mechanism requiring GTP (PubMed:15070734).
CC       {ECO:0000269|PubMed:15070734}.
CC   -!- CATALYTIC ACTIVITY: [Serine protease NS3]:
CC       Reaction=Leu is conserved at position P1 for all four cleavage sites.
CC         Alanine is found at position P1' of the NS4A-NS4B cleavage site,
CC         whereas serine is found at position P1' of the NS3-NS4A, NS4B-NS5A
CC         and NS5A-NS5B cleavage sites.; EC=3.4.21.113;
CC   -!- CATALYTIC ACTIVITY: [RNA-directed RNA polymerase]:
CC       Reaction=RNA(n) + a ribonucleoside 5'-triphosphate = RNA(n+1) +
CC         diphosphate; Xref=Rhea:RHEA:21248, Rhea:RHEA-COMP:14527, Rhea:RHEA-
CC         COMP:17342, ChEBI:CHEBI:33019, ChEBI:CHEBI:61557, ChEBI:CHEBI:140395;
CC         EC=2.7.7.48; Evidence={ECO:0000255|PROSITE-ProRule:PRU00539};
CC   -!- CATALYTIC ACTIVITY: [Serine protease NS3]:
CC       Reaction=a ribonucleoside 5'-triphosphate + H2O = a ribonucleoside 5'-
CC         diphosphate + phosphate + H(+); Xref=Rhea:RHEA:23680,
CC         ChEBI:CHEBI:15377, ChEBI:CHEBI:15378, ChEBI:CHEBI:43474,
CC         ChEBI:CHEBI:57930, ChEBI:CHEBI:61557; EC=3.6.1.15;
CC   -!- CATALYTIC ACTIVITY: [Serine protease NS3]:

CC         COMP:13936, Rhea:RHEA-COMP:17355, ChEBI:CHEBI:15377,
CC         ChEBI:CHEBI:15378, ChEBI:CHEBI:83062, ChEBI:CHEBI:138284,
CC         ChEBI:CHEBI:173118; EC=4.6.1.19;
CC         Evidence={ECO:0000250|UniProtKB:Q96662};
CC       PhysiologicalDirection=left-to-right; Xref=Rhea:RHEA:68053;
CC         Evidence={ECO:0000250|UniProtKB:Q96662};
CC   -!- CATALYTIC ACTIVITY: [E(rns) glycoprotein]:
CC       Reaction=a ribonucleotidyl-ribonucleotide-RNA = a 3'-end 2',3'-
CC         cyclophospho-ribonucleotide-RNA + a 5'-end dephospho-ribonucleoside-
CC         RNA; Xref=Rhea:RHEA:67796, Rhea:RHEA-COMP:10464, Rhea:RHEA-
CC         COMP:13936, Rhea:RHEA-COMP:17355, ChEBI:CHEBI:83064,
CC         ChEBI:CHEBI:138284, ChEBI:CHEBI:173118;
CC         Evidence={ECO:0000250|UniProtKB:Q96662};
CC       PhysiologicalDirection=left-to-right; Xref=Rhea:RHEA:67797;
CC         Evidence={ECO:0000250|UniProtKB:Q96662};
CC   -!- CATALYTIC ACTIVITY: [E(rns) glycoprotein]:
CC       Reaction=a 3'-end 2',3'-cyclophospho-ribonucleotide-RNA + H2O = a 3'-
CC         end 3'-phospho-ribonucleotide-RNA + H(+); Xref=Rhea:RHEA:68056,
CC         Rhea:RHEA-COMP:10463, Rhea:RHEA-COMP:10464, ChEBI:CHEBI:15377,
CC         ChEBI:CHEBI:15378, ChEBI:CHEBI:83062, ChEBI:CHEBI:83064;
CC         Evidence={ECO:0000250|UniProtKB:Q96662};
CC       PhysiologicalDirection=left-to-right; Xref=Rhea:RHEA:68057;
CC         Evidence={ECO:0000250|UniProtKB:Q96662};
CC   -!- ACTIVITY REGULATION: [E(rns) glycoprotein]: Inhibited by Zn(2+), which
CC       binds the catalytic site. {ECO:0000250|UniProtKB:Q96662}.
CC   -!- SUBUNIT: [E(rns) glycoprotein]: Homodimer (By similarity). E(rns)
CC       homodimer is disulfide-linked in other strains, but the cysteine
CC       involved in the bond is not conserved in isolate NADL (Probable).
CC       {ECO:0000250|UniProtKB:Q96662, ECO:0000305}.
CC   -!- SUBUNIT: [Envelope glycoprotein E1]: Homodimer; disulfide-linked (By
CC       similarity). Heterodimer with E1; disulfide-linked (By similarity).
CC       {ECO:0000250|UniProtKB:P19712}.
CC   -!- SUBUNIT: [Envelope glycoprotein E2]: Homodimer; disulfide-linked
CC       (PubMed:23569276). Heterodimer with E1; disulfide-linked (By
CC       similarity). {ECO:0000250|UniProtKB:P19712,
CC       ECO:0000269|PubMed:23569276}.
CC   -!- SUBUNIT: [Non-structural protein 4B]: Interacts with host IFIH1/MDA5;
CC       this interaction is involved in the inhibition of IFN-beta production.
CC       {ECO:0000269|PubMed:34097933}.

CC   -!- DOMAIN: [Envelope glycoprotein E1]: The transmembrane domain is

CC   -!- PTM: [E(rns) glycoprotein]: Heavily glycosylated.
CC       {ECO:0000250|UniProtKB:P19712}.
CC   -!- PTM: The viral RNA of pestiviruses is expressed as a single polyprotein
CC       which undergoes post-translational proteolytic processing resulting in
CC       the production of at least eleven individual proteins. The N-terminal
CC       protease cleaves itself from the nascent polyprotein autocatalytically
CC       and thereby generates the N-terminus of the adjacent viral capsid
CC       protein C (By similarity). {ECO:0000250}.
CC   -!- PTM: [Genome polyprotein]: Cleavage between E2 and p7 is partial.
CC   -!- MISCELLANEOUS: BVDV is divided in two types: cytopathic and non-
CC       cytopathic. Both types of viruses can be found in animals suffering
CC       from mucosal disease, as a cytopathic BVDV can develop from a non-
CC       cytopathic virus within the infected animal by deletions, mutations or
CC       insertions. Both types express uncleaved NS2-3, but cytopathic strains
CC       also express NS3. The cytopathic NADL strain contains an insertion (Jiv
CC       90) that potentiate the partial cleavage of NS2-3. Removal of this
CC       insertion in the NADL Jiv 90(-) strain results in a non-cytopathic
CC       strain in which NS2-3 remains uncleaved.
CC   -!- SIMILARITY: Belongs to the pestivirus polyprotein family.
CC       {ECO:0000305}.

RA   El Omari K., Iourin O., Harlos K., Grimes J.M., Stuart D.I.;
RT   "Structure of a pestivirus envelope glycoprotein E2 clarifies its role in
RT   cell entry.";
RL   Cell Rep. 3:30-35(2013).
CC   -!- FUNCTION: [N-terminal protease]: Leader cysteine autoprotease that
CC       cleaves itself from the nascent polyprotein during translation of the
CC       viral mRNA. Once released, plays a role in the inhibition of host
CC       innate immune response by interacting with host IRF3 and inducing its
CC       proteasomal degradation. {ECO:0000250|UniProtKB:P19711}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: [Capsid protein C]: Packages viral RNA to form a viral
CC       nucleocapsid and thereby protects viral RNA. Also plays a role in
CC       transcription regulation. Protects the incoming virus against IFN-
CC       induced effectors. {ECO:0000250|UniProtKB:P19712}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: [E(rns) glycoprotein]: Initial binding to target cell
CC       probably involves interaction of E(rns) with glycosaminoglycans (By
CC       similarity). Also possesses intrinsic ribonuclease (RNase) activity
CC       that can inhibit the production of type I interferon and assist in the
CC       development of persistent infections (By similarity).
CC       {ECO:0000250|UniProtKB:P19711, ECO:0000250|UniProtKB:Q96662}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: [Envelope glycoprotein E1]: E1 and/or E2 are probably
CC       responsible of cell attachment with CD46 and subsequent fusion after
CC       internalization of the virion by endocytosis.
CC       {ECO:0000250|UniProtKB:P19711}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: [Envelope glycoprotein E2]: E1 and/or E2 are probably
CC       responsible of cell attachment with CD46 and subsequent fusion after
CC       internalization of the virion by endocytosis (By similarity). Probably
CC       functions as a coeffector of fusion providing structural integrity to
CC       the fusion complex and possibly controlling exposure of the fusion
CC       motif in E1 (By similarity). {ECO:0000250|UniProtKB:P19711}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: [Viroporin p7]: Plays an essential role in the virus
CC       replication cycle by acting as a viroporin (By similarity). Forms ion
CC       conductive pores, which alters the cell permeability allowing the
CC       transport of ions and other small molecules (By similarity). Forms a
CC       leader sequence to properly orient NS2 in the membrane.
CC       {ECO:0000250|UniProtKB:P19712}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: [Non-structural protein 2-3]: Uncleaved NS2-3 is required for
CC       production of infectious virus.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: [Cysteine protease NS2]: Plays a role in the regulation of
CC       viral RNA replication. {ECO:0000250|UniProtKB:P19712}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: [Serine protease NS3]: Multifunctional protein that contains
CC       an N-terminal protease and a C-terminal helicase, playing essential
CC       roles in viral polyprotein processing and viral genome replication. The
CC       chymotrypsin-like serine protease activity utilizes NS4A as an
CC       essential cofactor and catalyzes the cleavage of the polyprotein
CC       leading to the release of NS4A, NS4B, NS5A, and NS5B. Interacts with
CC       NS5B to enhance RNA-dependent RNA polymerase activity.
CC       {ECO:0000250|UniProtKB:P19712}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: [Non-structural protein 4A]: Acts as a cofactor for the NS3
CC       protease activity. {ECO:0000250|UniProtKB:P19712}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: [Non-structural protein 4B]: Induces a specific membrane
CC       alteration that serves as a scaffold for the virus replication complex
CC       (By similarity). Plays a role in the inhibition of host innate immune
CC       response by inhibiting RIGI/IFIH1-mediated IFN-beta production (By
CC       similarity). {ECO:0000250|UniProtKB:P19711,
CC       ECO:0000250|UniProtKB:P19712}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: [RNA-directed RNA polymerase]: Replicates the viral (+) and
CC       (-) genome. Initiates the primer-independent RNA replication via a de
CC       novo mechanism requiring GTP (By similarity).
CC       {ECO:0000250|UniProtKB:P19711}.

CC         Alanine is found at position P1' of the NS4A-NS4B cleavage site,
CC         whereas serine is found at position P1' of the NS3-NS4A, NS4B-NS5A
CC         and NS5A-NS5B cleavage sites.; EC=3.4.21.113;

CC   -!- PTM: The viral RNA of pestiviruses is expressed as a single polyprotein
CC       which undergoes post-translational proteolytic processing resulting in
CC       the production of at least eleven individual proteins. The N-terminal
CC       protease cleaves itself from the nascent polyprotein autocatalytically
CC       and thereby generates the N-terminus of the adjacent viral capsid
CC       protein C. {ECO:0000250|UniProtKB:P19712}.
CC   -!- PTM: [Genome polyprotein]: Cleavage between E2 and p7 is partial.
CC   -!- MISCELLANEOUS: BVDV is divided in two types: cytopathic and non-
CC       cytopathic. Both types of viruses can be found in animals suffering
CC       from mucosal disease, as a cytopathic BVDV can develop from a non-
CC       cytopathic virus within the infected animal by deletions, mutations or
CC       insertions. Both types express uncleaved NS2-3, but cytopathic strains
CC       also express NS3.
CC   -!- SIMILARITY: Belongs to the pestivirus polyprotein family.
CC       {ECO:0000305}.

CC   -!- FUNCTION: Acts as a cofactor for the NS3 protease activity.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023576}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Leader cysteine autoprotease that cleaves itself from the
CC       nascent polyprotein during translation of the viral mRNA. Once
CC       released, plays a role in the inhibition of host innate immune response

CC   -!- FUNCTION: Acts as a cofactor for the NS3 protease activity.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023576}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Leader cysteine autoprotease that cleaves itself from the
CC       nascent polyprotein during translation of the viral mRNA. Once
CC       released, plays a role in the inhibition of host innate immune response
CC       by interacting with host IRF3 and inducing its proteasomal degradation.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023578}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Packages viral RNA to form a viral nucleocapsid and thereby
CC       protects viral RNA. Also plays a role in transcription regulation.
CC       Protects the incoming virus against IFN-induced effectors.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00034097}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Plays a role in the regulation of viral RNA replication.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023574}.
CC   -!- CATALYTIC ACTIVITY:

CC         ChEBI:CHEBI:15377, ChEBI:CHEBI:15378, ChEBI:CHEBI:30616,
CC         ChEBI:CHEBI:43474, ChEBI:CHEBI:456216; EC=3.6.4.13;
CC         Evidence={ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00047984};
CC   -!- CATALYTIC ACTIVITY:
CC       Reaction=Leu is conserved at position P1 for all four cleavage sites.
CC         Alanine is found at position P1' of the NS4A-NS4B cleavage site,
CC         whereas serine is found at position P1' of the NS3-NS4A, NS4B-NS5A
CC         and NS5A-NS5B cleavage sites.; EC=3.4.21.113;
CC         Evidence={ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00001160};

CC   -!- FUNCTION: Acts as a cofactor for the NS3 protease activity.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023576}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Leader cysteine autoprotease that cleaves itself from the
CC       nascent polyprotein during translation of the viral mRNA. Once
CC       released, plays a role in the inhibition of host innate immune response
CC       by interacting with host IRF3 and inducing its proteasomal degradation.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023578}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Packages viral RNA to form a viral nucleocapsid and thereby
CC       protects viral RNA. Also plays a role in transcription regulation.
CC       Protects the incoming virus against IFN-induced effectors.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00034097}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Plays a role in the regulation of viral RNA replication.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023574}.

CC       released, plays a role in the inhibition of host innate immune response

CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023578}.

CC   -!- FUNCTION: Acts as a cofactor for the NS3 protease activity.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023576}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Leader cysteine autoprotease that cleaves itself from the
CC       nascent polyprotein during translation of the viral mRNA. Once
CC       released, plays a role in the inhibition of host innate immune response
CC       by interacting with host IRF3 and inducing its proteasomal degradation.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023578}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Packages viral RNA to form a viral nucleocapsid and thereby
CC       protects viral RNA. Also plays a role in transcription regulation.
CC       Protects the incoming virus against IFN-induced effectors.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00034097}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Plays a role in the regulation of viral RNA replication.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023574}.

CC   -!- FUNCTION: Acts as a cofactor for the NS3 protease activity.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023576}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Leader cysteine autoprotease that cleaves itself from the
CC       nascent polyprotein during translation of the viral mRNA. Once
CC       released, plays a role in the inhibition of host innate immune response
CC       by interacting with host IRF3 and inducing its proteasomal degradation.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023578}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Packages viral RNA to form a viral nucleocapsid and thereby
CC       protects viral RNA. Also plays a role in transcription regulation.
CC       Protects the incoming virus against IFN-induced effectors.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00034097}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Plays a role in the regulation of viral RNA replication.

CC   -!- FUNCTION: Acts as a cofactor for the NS3 protease activity.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023576}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Leader cysteine autoprotease that cleaves itself from the
CC       nascent polyprotein during translation of the viral mRNA. Once
CC       released, plays a role in the inhibition of host innate immune response
CC       by interacting with host IRF3 and inducing its proteasomal degradation.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023578}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Packages viral RNA to form a viral nucleocapsid and thereby
CC       protects viral RNA. Also plays a role in transcription regulation.
CC       Protects the incoming virus against IFN-induced effectors.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00034097}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Plays a role in the regulation of viral RNA replication.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023574}.

CC   -!- FUNCTION: Acts as a cofactor for the NS3 protease activity.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023576}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: E1 and/or E2 are probably responsible of cell attachment with
CC       CD46 and subsequent fusion after internalization of the virion by
CC       endocytosis. Probably functions as a coeffector of fusion providing
CC       structural integrity to the fusion complex and possibly controlling
CC       exposure of the fusion motif in E1. {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00060156}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Induces a specific membrane alteration that serves as a
CC       scaffold for the virus replication complex. Plays a role in the
CC       inhibition of host innate immune response by inhibiting RIGI/IFIH1-
CC       mediated IFN-beta production. {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00056075}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Initial binding to target cell probably involves interaction
CC       of E(rns) with glycosaminoglycans. Also possesses intrinsic
CC       ribonuclease (RNase) activity that can inhibit the production of type I
CC       interferon and assist in the development of persistent infections.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00058575}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Leader cysteine autoprotease that cleaves itself from the
CC       nascent polyprotein during translation of the viral mRNA. Once
CC       released, plays a role in the inhibition of host innate immune response
CC       by interacting with host IRF3 and inducing its proteasomal degradation.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023578}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Multifunctional protein that contains an N-terminal protease
CC       and a C-terminal helicase, playing essential roles in viral polyprotein
CC       processing and viral genome replication. The chymotrypsin-like serine
CC       protease activity utilizes NS4A as an essential cofactor and catalyzes
CC       the cleavage of the polyprotein leading to the release of NS4A, NS4B,
CC       NS5A, and NS5B. Interacts with NS5B to enhance RNA-dependent RNA
CC       polymerase activity. {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00055401}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Packages viral RNA to form a viral nucleocapsid and thereby
CC       protects viral RNA. Also plays a role in transcription regulation.
CC       Protects the incoming virus against IFN-induced effectors.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00034097}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Plays a role in the regulation of viral RNA replication.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023574}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Plays an essential role in the virus replication cycle by
CC       acting as a viroporin. Forms ion conductive pores, which alters the
CC       cell permeability allowing the transport of ions and other small
CC       molecules. Forms a leader sequence to properly orient NS2 in the
CC       membrane. {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00059347}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Replicates the viral (+) and (-) genome. Initiates the
CC       primer-independent RNA replication via a de novo mechanism requiring
CC       GTP. {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00060359}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Uncleaved NS2-3 is required for production of infectious
CC       virus. {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00056976}.

CC   -!- FUNCTION: Acts as a cofactor for the NS3 protease activity.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023576}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Leader cysteine autoprotease that cleaves itself from the
CC       nascent polyprotein during translation of the viral mRNA. Once
CC       released, plays a role in the inhibition of host innate immune response
CC       by interacting with host IRF3 and inducing its proteasomal degradation.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023578}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Packages viral RNA to form a viral nucleocapsid and thereby
CC       protects viral RNA. Also plays a role in transcription regulation.
CC       Protects the incoming virus against IFN-induced effectors.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00034097}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Plays a role in the regulation of viral RNA replication.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023574}.

CC   -!- FUNCTION: Acts as a cofactor for the NS3 protease activity.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023576}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Leader cysteine autoprotease that cleaves itself from the
CC       nascent polyprotein during translation of the viral mRNA. Once
CC       released, plays a role in the inhibition of host innate immune response
CC       by interacting with host IRF3 and inducing its proteasomal degradation.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023578}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Packages viral RNA to form a viral nucleocapsid and thereby
CC       protects viral RNA. Also plays a role in transcription regulation.
CC       Protects the incoming virus against IFN-induced effectors.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00034097}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Plays a role in the regulation of viral RNA replication.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023574}.
CC   -!- CATALYTIC ACTIVITY:
CC       Reaction=ATP + H2O = ADP + phosphate + H(+); Xref=Rhea:RHEA:13065,
CC         ChEBI:CHEBI:15377, ChEBI:CHEBI:15378, ChEBI:CHEBI:30616,
CC         ChEBI:CHEBI:43474, ChEBI:CHEBI:456216; EC=3.6.4.13;
CC         Evidence={ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00047984};
CC   -!- CATALYTIC ACTIVITY:
CC       Reaction=Leu is conserved at position P1 for all four cleavage sites.
CC         Alanine is found at position P1' of the NS4A-NS4B cleavage site,
CC         whereas serine is found at position P1' of the NS3-NS4A, NS4B-NS5A
CC         and NS5A-NS5B cleavage sites.; EC=3.4.21.113;
CC         Evidence={ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00001160};
CC   -!- CATALYTIC ACTIVITY:

CC         Evidence={ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00047631};

CC   -!- FUNCTION: Leader cysteine autoprotease that cleaves itself from the

CC   -!- FUNCTION: Acts as a cofactor for the NS3 protease activity.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023576}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Leader cysteine autoprotease that cleaves itself from the
CC       nascent polyprotein during translation of the viral mRNA. Once
CC       released, plays a role in the inhibition of host innate immune response
CC       by interacting with host IRF3 and inducing its proteasomal degradation.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023578}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Packages viral RNA to form a viral nucleocapsid and thereby
CC       protects viral RNA. Also plays a role in transcription regulation.
CC       Protects the incoming virus against IFN-induced effectors.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00034097}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Plays a role in the regulation of viral RNA replication.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023574}.
CC   -!- CATALYTIC ACTIVITY:
CC       Reaction=ATP + H2O = ADP + phosphate + H(+); Xref=Rhea:RHEA:13065,
CC         ChEBI:CHEBI:15377, ChEBI:CHEBI:15378, ChEBI:CHEBI:30616,
CC         ChEBI:CHEBI:43474, ChEBI:CHEBI:456216; EC=3.6.4.13;
CC         Evidence={ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00047984};
CC   -!- CATALYTIC ACTIVITY:
CC       Reaction=Leu is conserved at position P1 for all four cleavage sites.
CC         Alanine is found at position P1' of the NS4A-NS4B cleavage site,
CC         whereas serine is found at position P1' of the NS3-NS4A, NS4B-NS5A
CC         and NS5A-NS5B cleavage sites.; EC=3.4.21.113;
CC         Evidence={ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00001160};
CC   -!- CATALYTIC ACTIVITY:
CC       Reaction=a ribonucleoside 5'-triphosphate + H2O = a ribonucleoside 5'-
CC         diphosphate + phosphate + H(+); Xref=Rhea:RHEA:23680,
CC         ChEBI:CHEBI:15377, ChEBI:CHEBI:15378, ChEBI:CHEBI:43474,
CC         ChEBI:CHEBI:57930, ChEBI:CHEBI:61557; EC=3.6.1.15;
CC         Evidence={ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00047631};
CC   -!- SUBUNIT: Homodimer; disulfide-linked. Heterodimer with E1; disulfide-
CC       linked. {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00046377}.

CC   -!- FUNCTION: Acts as a cofactor for the NS3 protease activity.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023576}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Leader cysteine autoprotease that cleaves itself from the
CC       nascent polyprotein during translation of the viral mRNA. Once
CC       released, plays a role in the inhibition of host innate immune response
CC       by interacting with host IRF3 and inducing its proteasomal degradation.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023578}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Packages viral RNA to form a viral nucleocapsid and thereby
CC       protects viral RNA. Also plays a role in transcription regulation.
CC       Protects the incoming virus against IFN-induced effectors.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00034097}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Plays a role in the regulation of viral RNA replication.

CC   -!- FUNCTION: Acts as a cofactor for the NS3 protease activity.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023576}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Leader cysteine autoprotease that cleaves itself from the
CC       nascent polyprotein during translation of the viral mRNA. Once
CC       released, plays a role in the inhibition of host innate immune response

RX   PubMed=24146623; DOI=10.1371/journal.ppat.1003704;
RA   Gottipati K., Ruggli N., Gerber M., Tratschin J.D., Benning M., Bellamy H.,
RA   Choi K.H.;
RT   "The structure of classical swine fever virus N(pro): a novel cysteine
RT   Autoprotease and zinc-binding protein involved in subversion of type I
RT   interferon induction.";
RL   PLoS Pathog. 9:e1003704-e1003704(2013).
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Acts as a cofactor for the NS3 protease activity.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023576}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Autoprotease that associates with the host chaperone JIV and
CC       cleaves the NS2-3 protein between NS2 and NS3. Also plays a role in the
CC       formation of infectious particles. {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00053892}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Induces a specific membrane alteration that serves as a
CC       scaffold for the virus replication complex. Antagonizes host cell
CC       apoptosis by interacting with host ferritin heavy chain. The ORF4
CC       protein physically binds host FTH1/FHC, resulting in the reduction of
CC       FTH1 protein levels in host cells. Reduction of FTH1 concentration
CC       further inhibits the accumulation of reactive oxygen in host cells,
CC       leading to reduced apoptosis. {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00057811}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Leader cysteine autoprotease that cleaves itself from the
CC       nascent polyprotein during translation of the viral mRNA. Once
CC       released, plays a role in the inhibition of host innate immune response
CC       by interacting with host IRF3 and inducing its proteasomal degradation.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023578}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Multifunctional protein that contains an N-terminal protease
CC       and a C-terminal helicase, playing essential roles in viral polyprotein
CC       processing and viral genome replication. The chymotrypsin-like serine
CC       protease activity utilizes NS4A as an essential cofactor and catalyzes
CC       the cleavage of the polyprotein leading to the release of NS4A, NS4B,
CC       NS5A, and NS5B. Plays a role in the inhibition of host NF-kappa-B
CC       activation by interacting with and inhibiting host TRAF6. Interacts
CC       with NS5B to enhance RNA-dependent RNA polymerase activity.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00055122}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Packages viral RNA to form a viral nucleocapsid and thereby
CC       protects viral RNA. Also plays a role in transcription regulation.
CC       Protects the incoming virus against IFN-induced effectors.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00034097}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Plays a role in cell attachment and subsequent fusion of
CC       viral and cellular membranes. Therefore, mediates together with
CC       envelope glycoprotein E1 the viral entry. Binds to host ADAM17 receptor
CC       for entry. Binds to host ANXA2 for entry. Binds to host MERTK for
CC       entry. {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00093354}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Plays a role in cell attachment and subsequent fusion of
CC       viral and cellular membranes. Therefore, mediates together with
CC       envelope glycoprotein E2 the viral entry.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00059170}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Plays a role in the regulation of viral RNA replication.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023574}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Plays a role in viral entry. Interacts with host RPSA that
CC       acts as a cellular attachment receptor for the virus. Also possesses
CC       intrinsic ribonuclease (RNase) activity that can inhibit the production
CC       of type I interferon and assist in the development of persistent
CC       infections. Cleaves preferentially NpU bonds. Binds to heparan sulfate
CC       on the host cells for entry. {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00093279}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Plays an essential role in the virus replication cycle by
CC       acting as a viroporin. Forms ion conductive pores, which alters the
CC       cell permeability allowing the transport of ions and other small
CC       molecules. {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00059234}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Regulates viral RNA replication by interacting with the 3'-
CC       untranslated region of viral RNA in a dose-dependent manner. At small
CC       concentrations promotes viral synthesis by interacting with the
CC       polymerase NS5B while at large concentrations, inhibits replication.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00055780}.
CC   -!- CATALYTIC ACTIVITY:
CC       Reaction=ATP + H2O = ADP + phosphate + H(+); Xref=Rhea:RHEA:13065,
CC         ChEBI:CHEBI:15377, ChEBI:CHEBI:15378, ChEBI:CHEBI:30616,
CC         ChEBI:CHEBI:43474, ChEBI:CHEBI:456216; EC=3.6.4.13;
CC         Evidence={ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00047984};
CC   -!- CATALYTIC ACTIVITY:
CC       Reaction=Leu is conserved at position P1 for all four cleavage sites.
CC         Alanine is found at position P1' of the NS4A-NS4B cleavage site,
CC         whereas serine is found at position P1' of the NS3-NS4A, NS4B-NS5A
CC         and NS5A-NS5B cleavage sites.; EC=3.4.21.113;
CC         Evidence={ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00001160};
CC   -!- CATALYTIC ACTIVITY:
CC       Reaction=a ribonucleoside 5'-triphosphate + H2O = a ribonucleoside 5'-
CC         diphosphate + phosphate + H(+); Xref=Rhea:RHEA:23680,
CC         ChEBI:CHEBI:15377, ChEBI:CHEBI:15378, ChEBI:CHEBI:43474,
CC         ChEBI:CHEBI:57930, ChEBI:CHEBI:61557; EC=3.6.1.15;
CC         Evidence={ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00047631};
CC   -!- SUBUNIT: Homodimer; disulfide-linked. Heterodimer with E1; disulfide-
CC       linked. Interacts with host TRX2. Interacts with host receptor ADAM17
CC       (via metalloproteinase domain); this interaction allows binding and
CC       probably entry of the virus into the host cell. Interacts with host
CC       ANXA2; this interaction allows binding and probably entry of the virus
CC       into the host cell. Interacts with host MERTK; this interaction allows
CC       binding and probably entry of the virus into the host cell.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00093470}.
CC   -!- SUBUNIT: Homodimer; disulfide-linked. Interacts with host RPSA.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00064076}.
CC   -!- SUBUNIT: Interacts (via N-terminus) with host SP1; this interaction
CC       induces proteasomal degradation of SP1 with subsequent down-regulation
CC       of HDAC1 and ISG15 expression thereby counteracting the host innate
CC       immunity. Interacts (via C-terminus) with host IRF3.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00061753}.
CC   -!- SUBUNIT: Interacts with NS5A; this interaction promotes viral
CC       replication. {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00066206}.
CC   -!- SUBUNIT: Interacts with RNA-directed RNA polymerase. Interacts with
CC       host RSAD2; this interaction inhibits viral replication.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00064052}.
CC   -!- SUBUNIT: Interacts with host OS9. {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00064522}.
CC   -!- SUBUNIT: Interacts with host RAB5, this interaction facilitates the
CC       formation of NS4B-related complex. Interacts with host FTH1; this
CC       interaction plays a positive role in viral anti-apoptosis.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00063660}.
CC   -!- SUBUNIT: Interacts with host TRAF6; this interaction inhibits host NF-
CC       kappa-B pathway. Interacts with NS5B; this interaction enhances RNA-
CC       dependent RNA polymerase activity. Interacts with protein NS4A.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00062832}.
CC   -!- INTERACTION:

CC       Q68871; O00165: HAX1; Xeno; NbExp=3; IntAct=EBI-12522528, EBI-357001;
CC       Q68871; Q764M6: IRF3; Xeno; NbExp=5; IntAct=EBI-12522528, EBI-12512266;
CC       Q68871; A0ZVR0: IRF7; Xeno; NbExp=5; IntAct=EBI-12522528, EBI-12517858;
CC   -!- SUBCELLULAR LOCATION: Host cell surface
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00004426}. Host cytoplasm

CC   -!- FUNCTION: Acts as a cofactor for the NS3 protease activity.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023576}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Leader cysteine autoprotease that cleaves itself from the
CC       nascent polyprotein during translation of the viral mRNA. Once
CC       released, plays a role in the inhibition of host innate immune response
CC       by interacting with host IRF3 and inducing its proteasomal degradation.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023578}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Packages viral RNA to form a viral nucleocapsid and thereby
CC       protects viral RNA. Also plays a role in transcription regulation.
CC       Protects the incoming virus against IFN-induced effectors.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00034097}.
CC   -!- FUNCTION: Plays a role in the regulation of viral RNA replication.
CC       {ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00023574}.
CC   -!- CATALYTIC ACTIVITY:

CC         ChEBI:CHEBI:15377, ChEBI:CHEBI:15378, ChEBI:CHEBI:30616,
CC         ChEBI:CHEBI:43474, ChEBI:CHEBI:456216; EC=3.6.4.13;
CC         Evidence={ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00047984};
CC   -!- CATALYTIC ACTIVITY:
CC       Reaction=Leu is conserved at position P1 for all four cleavage sites.
CC         Alanine is found at position P1' of the NS4A-NS4B cleavage site,
CC         whereas serine is found at position P1' of the NS3-NS4A, NS4B-NS5A
CC         and NS5A-NS5B cleavage sites.; EC=3.4.21.113;
CC         Evidence={ECO:0000256|ARBA:ARBA00001160};
